36:["$","p",null,{"children":"Systems that succeed start with the intended experience (aesthetic) and design mechanics to serve it. Systems that fail start with cool mechanics and try to find a use for them."}]
37:["$","p",null,{"children":"This is the MDA framework's reversal:"}]
38:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Players experience:"}]," Aesthetics → Dynamics → Mechanics"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Designers create:"}]," Mechanics → Dynamics → Aesthetics"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"But designers should START with:"}]," Aesthetics (what experience?) → then design Mechanics/Dynamics to achieve it"]}],"\n"]}]

46:["$","p",null,{"children":["D&D and Civilization are foundational for a reason: they ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"defined categories"}]," and showed designers what's possible at scale. They're not the only important systems, but they're historically necessary."]}]
47:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"D&D"}]," (1974 to present) demonstrates:"]}]
48:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"How systems survive radical redesign (five complete editions)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"What must stay constant (six attributes, levels, hit points)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"How mechanical changes cascade into different experiences (3e vs. 5e)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"The limits of complexity (3.5e's baroque optimization vs. 5e's elegant simplicity)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"That player identity matters more than mechanical elegance"}],"\n"]}]
49:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Civilization"}]," (1991 to present) demonstrates:"]}]
4a:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"How systems manage complexity over time (Civ I simple → Civ IV complex → Civ V simplified → Civ VI smartly complex)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"That spatial/visual complexity feels different from numerical complexity"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"How feedback loops create compulsion (\"one more turn\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"That multiple paths to success creates replayability"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"How interface IS part of the system (adjacency bonuses in Civ VI changed strategy)"}],"\n"]}]
4b:["$","p",null,{"children":"These aren't equal to all other systems—they're foundational because they showed categories of problems and solutions that every other designer builds from or reacts against."}]
4c:["$","h3",null,{"className":"flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2","id":"dds-50-year-evolution-what-systems-must-manage","children":[["$","a",null,{"data-card":"","href":"#dds-50-year-evolution-what-systems-must-manage","className":"peer","children":"D&D's 50-Year Evolution: What Systems Must Manage"}],["$","svg",null,{"xmlns":"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg","width":24,"height":24,"viewBox":"0 0 24 24","fill":"none","stroke":"currentColor","strokeWidth":2,"strokeLinecap":"round","strokeLinejoin":"round","className":"lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100","aria-label":"Link to section","children":[[["$","path","1cjeqo",{"d":"M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"}],["$","path","19qd67",{"d":"M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"}]],"$undefined"]}]]}]
4d:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"The core pattern:"}]," D&D shows how designers respond to specific problems each edition identifies."]}]
4e:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"OD&D → AD&D (1974-1977):"}]," Players needed consistent rulings for tournament play. Solution: Codify everything. Lesson: Systematization enables markets but constrains emergent play."]}]
4f:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"AD&D 2e → 3e (1989-2000):"}]," Every resolution mechanic was different (Thac0 for combat, ability checks variable, saves on tables). Solution: Unified d20 system. Lesson: One elegant core mechanic unifies experience, but invites endless expansion."]}]
50:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"3.5e → 4e (2008):"}]," Martial classes were underpowered compared to casters; system had grown baroque. Solution: Powers system for everyone, tactical grid emphasis. Result: Technically superior but commercially failed (Pathfinder outsold it). Lesson: Mechanical excellence alone is insufficient; you must preserve what players love."]}]
51:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"4e → 5e (2014):"}]," 4e felt like a board game, not D&D. Solution: Return to tradition with modern design (advantage/disadvantage, bounded accuracy). Result: Most successful edition ever. Lesson: Sometimes simplification > innovation."]}]
52:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"What D&D teaches about systems:"}]}]
53:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Core identity matters more than mechanical perfection (six attributes remained constant through five editions)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Can't fix problems by violating identity (4e proved this)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Simplicity, carefully designed, beats complex optimization"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Accessibility expands audiences (5e's triumph)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Systems evolve in response to specific problems, but solutions must preserve purpose"}],"\n"]}]
54:["$","h3",null,{"className":"flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2","id":"civilizations-25-year-progression-complexity-and-pacing","children":[["$","a",null,{"data-card":"","href":"#civilizations-25-year-progression-complexity-and-pacing","className":"peer","children":"Civilization's 25-Year Progression: Complexity and Pacing"}],["$","svg",null,{"xmlns":"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg","width":24,"height":24,"viewBox":"0 0 24 24","fill":"none","stroke":"currentColor","strokeWidth":2,"strokeLinecap":"round","strokeLinejoin":"round","className":"lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100","aria-label":"Link to section","children":[[["$","path","1cjeqo",{"d":"M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"}],["$","path","19qd67",{"d":"M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"}]],"$undefined"]}]]}]
55:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"The parallel evolution:"}]," Civilization shows what happens when you manage complexity in a computed medium (no human adjudication required)."]}]
56:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"I → II → III → IV:"}]," Each added systems. Depth increased, tedium increased."]}]
57:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"IV → V:"}]," Radical simplification. Removed Religion, Espionage, Corporations. Changed fundamental interaction (One Unit Per Tile instead of stacking). Hexagonal grid instead of square. Reception: Divisive. Hardcore players hated simplification. New players loved accessibility."]}]
58:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"V → VI:"}]," Managed complexity return. Districts (spatial complexity) instead of numerical optimization. Eureka moments (guiding progression instead of pure freedom). Result: Depth without tedium."]}]
59:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"What Civilization teaches about systems:"}]}]
5a:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Complexity is a budget; spend wisely"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Spatial/visual complexity (districts) feels better than numerical complexity (spreadsheets)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Positive feedback loops create compulsion (cities grow → more production → faster growth)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Near-miss losses drive replays (\"if only I'd built that three turns earlier\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Short-term goals (units finishing soon) + long-term planning (fifty turns to victory) creates \"one more turn\" feeling"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"UI/interface matters as much as mechanics"}],"\n"]}]

7a:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Critical Distinction: Genre vs Dressing"}]}]
7b:["$","p",null,{"children":"Context has two layers that must be distinguished:"}]
7c:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Genre (load-bearing structure):"}]}]

be:["$","p",null,{"children":"The MDA framework, formalized by Hunicke, LeBlanc, and Zubek (2004), provides essential vocabulary:"}]
bf:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mechanics:"}]," The rules, data, algorithms (what designers directly control)"]}]
c0:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Dynamics:"}]," The runtime behavior (what emerges when mechanics interact and players engage)"]}]
c1:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Aesthetics:"}]," The emotional responses players experience (what players actually feel)"]}]
c2:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Critical insight:"}]," Design flows ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mechanics → Dynamics → Aesthetics"}]," (cause to effect), but designers should ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"START with Aesthetics"}]," (desired experience), then work backward to design mechanics that create it."]}]

fc:["$","p",null,{"children":["A core loop is ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"the smallest complete circuit of action, feedback, reward, and motivation that brings the player back to take action again."}]," This is what players do over and over, sometimes hundreds of times per session. If your core loop isn't satisfying, nothing else matters."]}]
fd:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Core loop structure:"}]}]
fe:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Action:"}]," Player does something"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Feedback:"}]," System responds immediately"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Reward:"}]," Player receives outcome (success, progress, information, emotion)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Motivation:"}]," Outcome creates desire to take action again"]}],"\n"]}]
ff:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Examples across different systems:"}]}]
100:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Wordle:"}]}]
101:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Guess word → See colored feedback → Adjust strategy → Guess again"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Loop completes in seconds, repeats 6 times per puzzle"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Reward: Information (which letters work) + Progress (closer to solution)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Motivation: Desire to solve before running out of guesses"}],"\n"]}]
102:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Civilization:"}]}]
103:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Choose action → See immediate effect → Plan next turn → Choose action again"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Loop completes in 30-60 seconds, repeats hundreds of times"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Reward: Progress (city grows, unit builds, research advances)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Motivation: \"One more turn\" compulsion"}],"\n"]}]
104:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"D&D Combat:"}]}]
105:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Declare action → Roll dice → Resolve outcome → Next turn"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Loop completes in 1-3 minutes, repeats 20-40 times per combat"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Reward: Tactical success, resource management, narrative progression"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Motivation: Desire to survive, win, see what happens next"}],"\n"]}]
106:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Critical distinction: Tasks end. Loops continue."}]}]
107:["$","p",null,{"children":"Traditional task-completion thinking: \"User completes form → System saves data → Done.\""}]
108:["$","p",null,{"children":"Core loop thinking: \"Player acts → System responds with satisfaction + hook → Player wants to act again.\""}]
109:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Design implications:"}]}]
10a:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Every system element should either enhance or protect the core loop"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"If a mechanic breaks the loop's rhythm, it damages engagement"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Different loops serve different purposes (Wordle: puzzle-solving, Civ: expansion, D&D: tactical drama)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"The loop must be satisfying even when repeated hundreds of times"}],"\n"]}]

162:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Design principles for investment matching:"}]}]

required"}]}],"\n",["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Don't market deep games as casual"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Don't promise \"5-minute sessions\" if mastery 164:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Integration with flow theory:"}]}]
165:["$","p",null,{"children":"Flow state requirements DEPEND on energy state:"}]
166:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Exhausted player: Flow happens quickly (1-2 minutes) with simple challenges"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Dedicated player: Flow takes longer (5-10 minutes) but sustains longer with complex challenges"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Same challenge level feels different based on energy state"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Design flow curves for your target energy state"}],"\n"]}]

16c:["$","h2",null,{"className":"flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2","id":"part-7-common-design-mistakes","children":[["$","a",null,{"data-card":"","href":"#part-7-common-design-mistakes","className":"peer","children":"Part 7: Common Design Mistakes"}],["$","svg",null,{"xmlns":"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg","width":24,"height":24,"viewBox":"0 0 24 24","fill":"none","stroke":"currentColor","strokeWidth":2,"strokeLinecap":"round","strokeLinejoin":"round","className":"lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100","aria-label":"Link to section","children":[[["$","path","1cjeqo",{"d":"M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"}],["$","path","19qd67",{"d":"M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"}]],"$undefined"]}]]}]
16d:["$","p",null,{"children":"Understanding common failures helps avoid them."}]
16e:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"1. Starting with Mechanics Instead of Purpose"}]}]
16f:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Symptom:"}]," \"I have this cool dice mechanic! What game should I make?\""]}]
170:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Result:"}]," Solution looking for problem. Mechanics don't serve purpose because purpose came second."]}]
171:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Example:"}]," D&D 4e started with \"balanced powers system\" without asking \"does this serve D&D's purpose?\""]}]
172:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fix:"}]," Start with experience goal, then design mechanics to create it."]}]
173:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"2. Feature Creep and Unmotivated Complexity"}]}]
174:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Symptom:"}]," \"This system needs more depth! Add crafting! Add factions! Add weather!\""]}]
175:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Result:"}]," System becomes baroque. Unmotivated complexity becomes tedium."]}]
176:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Example:"}]," D&D 3.5e's feat chains. Technically deep, but optimization became burden, not joy."]}]
177:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fix:"}]," Every system must serve the core experience. If you can't connect it back, cut it."]}]
178:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"3. Ignoring Parameters"}]}]
179:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Symptom:"}]," Designers focus on mechanics and ignore tuning. \"The game feels off but the mechanics are right.\""]}]
17a:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Result:"}]," Parameters are wrong. Same mechanic, wrong configuration."]}]
17b:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Example:"}]," Resource scarcity too low → nothing threatens you → tension gone. Could be fixed by parameter change, not mechanics redesign."]}]
17c:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fix:"}]," Before redesigning mechanics, try tuning parameters: scarcity, speed, pressure, limits, recovery."]}]
17d:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"4. Treating Context as Cosmetic"}]}]
17e:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Symptom:"}]," \"We'll add story/flavor later.\""]}]
17f:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Result:"}]," Context should frame what mechanics mean. Without it, mechanics are abstract, unfelt."]}]
180:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Example:"}]," Same card game with \"researching magic\" theme vs. \"managing resources\" theme feels completely different."]}]
181:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fix:"}]," Choose context first. It determines what mechanics mean."]}]
182:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"5. Violating Core Identity"}]}]
183:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Symptom:"}]," Trying to fix problems by changing fundamental nature."]}]
184:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Result:"}]," You alienate core audience. See D&D 4e."]}]
185:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Example:"}]," \"Barbarians feel weak compared to spellcasters\" → \"Let's give everyone powers\" → Now barbarians are spellcasters, which isn't what players wanted."]}]
186:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fix:"}]," Know what your system IS. Problems should be solved within identity, not by violating it."]}]
187:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"6. No Feedback Loop"}]}]
188:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Symptom:"}]," Players can't understand causality. Why did they lose? What would work better?"]}]
189:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Result:"}]," Frustration. Players can't improve. Retention plummets."]}]
18a:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Example:"}]," Opaque mechanics without explanation. (Exception: Cultist Simulator does this intentionally as discovery mechanic)"]}]
18b:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fix:"}]," Most games need clear feedback. Players should understand cause and effect."]}]
18c:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"7. Wrong Investment Level for Audience"}]}]
18d:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Symptom:"}]," Designed for exhausted casual players, but demands high-attention play. Or promised depth for dedicated players but delivered shallow mechanics."]}]
18e:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Result:"}]," Energy state mismatch. Game is wonderful for wrong audience, miserable for target audience."]}]
18f:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Example:"}]," Complex optimization-heavy game marketed as \"relaxing cozy game\" - exhausted players bounce off. Or \"hardcore strategy game\" that's mastered in 10 hours - dedicated players leave disappointed."]}]
190:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fix:"}]}]
191:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Know your audience's target energy state"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Design investment level to match"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Be honest in marketing about what you demand"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Match payoff to investment required"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Don't try to serve all energy states equally"}],"\n"]}]
192:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"8. Exploitation Over Engagement (Ethical Failure)"}]}]
193:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Symptom:"}]," Using psychological manipulation to extract time/money rather than create genuine enjoyment."]}]
194:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Result:"}]," Short-term metrics improve, long-term trust destroyed. Players feel used, not entertained."]}]
195:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Examples of dark patterns:"}]}]
196:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Punishing missed login streaks without forgiveness mechanics (creating anxiety, not motivation)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Deliberately confusing monetization (hiding real costs, exploiting cognitive biases)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Endless engagement hooks designed to prevent stopping (no natural endpoints)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Preying on FOMO (fear of missing out) with limited-time pressure tactics"}],"\n"]}]
197:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Why this fails:"}]}]
198:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Violates player trust and wellbeing"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Creates resentment, not loyalty"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Damages reputation and community"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Ethically indefensible even if profitable"}],"\n"]}]
199:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Good design alternative:"}]}]
19a:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Streak freezes and rest days (respect player autonomy)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Clear value propositions (transparent costs and benefits)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Natural session endings (respecting player time)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Optional FOMO, not mandatory (events are bonuses, not punishments for absence)"}],"\n"]}]
19b:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"The fundamental principle: Design should enhance players' lives, not exploit their psychology."}]}]
19c:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fix:"}]," Engagement should make players feel good about their time spent. If players feel manipulated, you've failed ethically even if you've succeeded commercially. Respect player time, money, and wellbeing."]}]
19d:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"9. Incoherent Configuration"}]}]
19e:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Symptom:"}]," Feels like different games stapled together. Players confused about what matters. Mechanics say one thing, context says another."]}]
19f:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Result:"}]," Players don't know what the system wants them to do. Experience feels inconsistent."]}]
1a0:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Example:"}]," D&D 4e - mechanics said \"tactical board game,\" context said \"D&D RPG,\" players got confused."]}]
1a1:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fix:"}]," Everything must serve the same aesthetic. If something doesn't fit, cut it or change it. Configuration is where system emerges from mechanics."]}]
1a2:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"10. Ignoring Pacing"}]}]
1a3:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Symptom:"}]," Early game great, late game tedious. No peaks and valleys (constant intensity burns out). Wrong rhythm for context (horror needs breathing room)."]}]
1a4:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Result:"}]," Players engage early, quit when pacing breaks."]}]
1a5:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Example:"}]," Civ IV late game micromanagement tedium. Same intensity for 4 hours causes burnout."]}]
1a6:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fix:"}]," Pacing transforms mechanics. Same combat system feels different at different pacing. Design escalation curves, rest cycles, pressure valves."]}]
1a7:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"11. Building for Wrong Aesthetic (System Selection Error)"}]}]
1a8:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Symptom:"}]," Using a system designed for one aesthetic to deliver a different aesthetic."]}]
1a9:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Result:"}]," System functions don't support intended experience. Players follow mechanics over intended fiction."]}]
1aa:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Example:"}]," Using D&D 5e for mystery investigation."]}]
1ab:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Why it fails:"}]}]
1ac:["$","div",null,{"className":"relative overflow-auto prose-no-margin my-6","children":["$","table",null,{"children":[["$","thead",null,{"children":["$","tr",null,{"children":[["$","th",null,{"children":"What Mystery Needs"}],["$","th",null,{"children":"What D&D Provides"}],["$","th",null,{"children":"Result"}]]}]}],["$","tbody",null,{"children":[["$","tr",null,{"children":[["$","td",null,{"children":"Information management (core clues guaranteed)"}],["$","td",null,{"children":"Roll-to-find (can miss clues)"}],["$","td",null,{"children":"Investigation stalls"}]]}],["$","tr",null,{"children":[["$","td",null,{"children":"Investigation mechanics"}],["$","td",null,{"children":"Combat mechanics"}],["$","td",null,{"children":"Players solve problems with violence"}]]}],["$","tr",null,{"children":[["$","td",null,{"children":"Detective character focus"}],["$","td",null,{"children":"Generic adventurer creation"}],["$","td",null,{"children":"Incompatible characters allowed"}]]}],["$","tr",null,{"children":[["$","td",null,{"children":"Deduction as core loop"}],["$","td",null,{"children":"Combat as core loop"}],["$","td",null,{"children":"Mechanics reward wrong behavior"}]]}]]}]]}]}]
1ad:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"The problem isn't that D&D is bad—it's that D&D is designed for different aesthetic (heroic combat adventure, not intellectual deduction)."}]}]
1ae:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"How to detect this mistake:"}]}]
1af:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Step 1: Identify required system functions for your aesthetic"}]}]
1b0:["$","p",null,{"children":"For mystery aesthetic:"}]
1b1:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Information management (critical)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"State persistence (for continuity)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Character-aesthetic alignment (investigators only)"}],"\n"]}]
1b2:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Step 2: Check if chosen system provides these functions"}]}]
1b3:["$","p",null,{"children":"D&D 5e for mystery:"}]
1b4:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Information management: ❌ (roll-to-find breaks flow)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"State persistence: ⚠️ (manual notes only)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Character-aesthetic alignment: ❌ (allows any character type)"}],"\n"]}]
1b5:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Verdict:"}]," 2 of 3 critical functions missing/broken. Wrong system."]}]
1b6:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Step 3: Evaluate configuration coherence"}]}]
1b7:["$","p",null,{"children":"Ask: \"Do mechanics align with intended context?\""}]
1b8:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"D&D mechanics: Combat, tactical positioning, resource management"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Mystery context: Investigation, deduction, clue interpretation"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Result: ❌ Incoherent (combat mechanics in investigation context)"}],"\n"]}]
1b9:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Step 4: Predict player behavior"}]}]
1ba:["$","p",null,{"children":"Players follow what mechanics reward, not what context suggests:"}]
1bb:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"D&D rewards: Violence, tactical positioning, resource optimization"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Mystery needs: Investigation, deduction, careful questioning"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Prediction: Players will solve mysteries through violence (killing suspects, looting clues from corpses)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Observed: Exactly this happens in play"}],"\n"]}]
1bc:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fix: Choose system that matches aesthetic"}]}]
1bd:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Option 1: Use purpose-built system"}]}]
1be:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Mystery aesthetic → Gumshoe (or similar)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Tactical combat → D&D, Pathfinder"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Social intrigue → Burning Wheel, PbtA social games"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Horror → Call of Cthulhu, Dread"}],"\n"]}]
1bf:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Option 2: Heavily modify system"}]}]
1c0:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Replace broken functions (new information management rules)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Restrict character creation (only investigators)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Add missing mechanics (investigation system)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Warning: This is essentially designing new system"}],"\n"]}]
1c1:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Option 3: Acknowledge constraints, design around them"}]}]
1c2:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Accept system limitations"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Use strengths (D&D combat for action scenes)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Work within constraints (mysteries as side content, not main focus)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Set appropriate expectations"}],"\n"]}]
1c3:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"When you MUST use wrong system (brand requirements, player investment):"}]}]
1c4:["$","p",null,{"children":"Be explicit about limitations:"}]
1c5:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"This system isn't designed for mystery, so we'll house-rule investigation\""}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Combat will appear more than typical mystery game because that's what system does well\""}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Your characters should be combat-capable investigators, not pure detectives\""}],"\n"]}]
1c6:["$","p",null,{"children":"Supplement heavily:"}]
1c7:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Add information management rules"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Create investigation subsystem"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Provide character creation guidance"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Use LLM to compensate for missing functions"}],"\n"]}]
1c8:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Framework principle:"}]}]
1c9:["$","blockquote",null,{"children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"children":"Systems are designed for specific aesthetics. Using a system for different aesthetic is like using hammer for screws—technically possible but frustrating. Choose the right tool, or design a new one."}],"\n"]}]
1ca:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Test:"}]," For each critical function your aesthetic requires, verify your chosen system provides it. If 2+ critical functions are missing or broken, you need a different system."]}]

206:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Two approaches to critical information:"}]}]
207:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Traditional RPG Model (D&D):"}]}]
208:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"All information gated by player action + dice rolls"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Missing information = investigation stalls"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"GM must improvise or railroad to maintain progress"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Problem: Core information can be missed"}],"\n"]}]
209:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mystery Game Model (Gumshoe):"}]}]
20a:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Distinguish core information (necessary) from optional (enrichment)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Core information: Automatically found when investigating relevant locations"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Optional information: Requires resource expenditure or special circumstances"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Solution: Progress guaranteed, challenge shifts to interpretation"}],"\n"]}]
20b:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Examples:"}]}]
20c:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Gumshoe (mystery games):"}],"\nCore clues distributed automatically when in right location with right skill. Additional clues cost investigation points. Ensures forward progress while rewarding thorough investigation."]}]
20d:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Blades in the Dark:"}],"\nFlashbacks let players reveal information retroactively (\"Actually, I prepared for this earlier...\"). Information emerges through play, not pre-planning."]}]
20e:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Cultist Simulator:"}],"\nExtreme opacity. Information must be discovered through experimentation. Frustrating for some, deeply satisfying for others. Intentional design choice."]}]
20f:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Traditional D&D:"}],"\nGM holds all secrets, players must ask right questions. Can lead to \"guess what the GM is thinking\" frustration. Information management is GM burden, not system function."]}]

211:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Consistent world state (remembers what players know vs don't know)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Fair-play mystery generation (clues are logically consistent)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Adaptive revelation (adjusts pacing based on player progress)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Dynamic redistribution (core information appears wherever players investigate)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Challenge: Avoiding railroading, preserving player agency in discovery"}],"\n"]}]

296:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Real Example (Mystery):"}]}]
297:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"What happened:"}]," Player created \"cowardly warrior focused on survival and payment\" for mystery game."]}]
298:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Why this broke the aesthetic:"}]}]
299:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Mystery aesthetic requires caring about \"being correct\" (intellectual vindication)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Character cared about \"getting paid and surviving\" (pragmatic completion)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["Red herrings (essential mystery element) had no meaning:","\n",["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"For detective: Following false lead = wasted time = failure"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"For cowardly warrior: Following false lead = still got paid = success"}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Character was well-designed, just wrong game"}],"\n"]}]

29b:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Solution: Filter Through Character Creation"}]}]
29c:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Principle:"}]," Character creation should guide players toward characters that enable the intended aesthetic, not allow infinite options."]}]
29d:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Implementation approaches:"}]}]
29e:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"1. Limited Archetypes (Restrictive)"}]}]
29f:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Provide only character types compatible with aesthetic"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Mystery game: Detective, Researcher, Reporter, Forensic Expert"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"No option to create incompatible types"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Pros: Guarantees fit, clear expectations"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Cons: Feels restrictive, reduces player freedom"}],"\n"]}]
2a0:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"2. Mandatory Drives/Motivations (Guided)"}]}]
2a1:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"All characters must have mechanical motivation aligned with aesthetic"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Mystery game: Every character has \"Drive\" (why they solve mysteries)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Drive provides mechanical benefits when pursuing aesthetic"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Examples: \"Protect innocent,\" \"Uncover truth,\" \"Advance career,\" \"Prove yourself\""}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Pros: Ensures investment, maintains some freedom"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Cons: Requires careful design of drives"}],"\n"]}]
2a2:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"3. Explicit Requirements (Educational)"}]}]
2a3:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Character creation clearly states: \"This game requires X type of character\""}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Explains why certain types won't work"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Provides examples of appropriate vs. inappropriate"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Trusts players to self-select"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Pros: Maintains freedom, educates players"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Cons: Some players will ignore guidance"}],"\n"]}]

317:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Proposed spectrum:"}]}]
318:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"High Automation (Mechanical, Consistent):"}]}]
319:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Scene counters (\"villain acts after scene 6\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Clue thresholds (\"when 4 clues found, Act 2 begins\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Automatic resource depletion"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Pros: Consistent, fair, predictable, no GM skill required"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Cons: Inflexible, can feel mechanical, can't adapt to circumstances"}],"\n"]}]
31a:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Medium Automation (Player-Influenced, Variable):"}]}]
31b:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Complication tables (roll after each scene)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Investigation point economy (players control pace through spending)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Danger from actions (player choices trigger complications)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Pros: Variable, player agency, some randomness, some consistency"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Cons: Can be too unpredictable, requires system design"}],"\n"]}]
31c:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Low Automation (GM Judgment, Flexible):"}]}]
31d:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"GM decides when to escalate based on pace"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Complications introduced when dramatically appropriate"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Flexible adjustment to player progress"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Pros: Maximally flexible, can adapt perfectly, feels natural"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Cons: Requires skilled GM, inconsistent between GMs, can feel arbitrary"}],"\n"]}]
31e:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Evidence so far:"}]}]
31f:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"✓ Mystery pacing (Scenario 3): Proposed using scene counter (high) + point economy (medium) + LLM monitoring"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"? Time-constrained pacing (Scenario 1): Untested—does 2-hour session need high automation?"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"? Open-world pacing (Scenario 2 or others): Untested—does exploration need low automation?"}],"\n"]}]
320:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"What would validate:"}]," If different aesthetics consistently benefit from different automation levels."]}]
321:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"What would invalidate:"}]," If automation level doesn't correlate with aesthetic success, or if same aesthetic works equally well at all levels."]}]
322:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Design implications if validated:"}]}]
323:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Mystery/horror → High automation (consistent dread, fair investigation)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Exploration/sandbox → Low automation (flexibility for player-driven discovery)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Action/tactical → Medium automation (player choices matter, but structure exists)"}],"\n"]}]
324:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"LLM consideration:"}]," LLM could operate at medium automation level—monitoring pace, suggesting escalations, but GM approves. Combines consistency with flexibility."]}]

3a9:["$","h3",null,{"className":"flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2","id":"how-to-use-this-section","children":[["$","a",null,{"data-card":"","href":"#how-to-use-this-section","className":"peer","children":"How to Use This Section"}],["$","svg",null,{"xmlns":"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg","width":24,"height":24,"viewBox":"0 0 24 24","fill":"none","stroke":"currentColor","strokeWidth":2,"strokeLinecap":"round","strokeLinejoin":"round","className":"lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100","aria-label":"Link to section","children":[[["$","path","1cjeqo",{"d":"M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"}],["$","path","19qd67",{"d":"M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"}]],"$undefined"]}]]}]
3aa:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"For designers:"}]}]
3ab:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Hypotheses: Interesting patterns that might help your design, but verify for your specific case"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Research questions: Deeper problems that don't have clear answers yet"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Validated findings: Safe to rely on these principles, they're confirmed"}],"\n"]}]

3b0:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Think of this as:"}]," The \"working notes\" or \"reader's guide\" showing framework development process, not just final product. Makes framework scientific and transparent about confidence levels."]}]
3b1:["$","hr",null,{}]
3b2:["$","p",null,{"children":["A game system is not its mechanics. It's the ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"designed interplay of mechanics, parameters, context, and pacing configured to serve a specific intended experience through specific functions."}]]}]
3b3:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"What we learned from studying actual systems:"}]}]
3b4:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From D&D:"}]," Identity matters. Systems survive if they know what they are. Mechanical \"improvements\" fail if they violate identity."]}]
3b5:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From Civilization:"}]," Complexity must be managed. Spatial complexity feels better than numerical. Feedback loops create compulsion. Multiple victory paths create replayability."]}]
3b6:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From PbtA:"}]," Simple core mechanics enable more variation. Configuration matters more than mechanics. Same engine can serve opposite genres through reconfiguration."]}]
3b7:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From MDA:"}]," Start with aesthetics (experience goal), work backward to mechanics. Not mechanics-first. We control mechanics, we predict dynamics, but players come back for aesthetics."]}]
3b8:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From Ludology:"}]," Simple rules can produce complex emergent behavior. Systems interact in unpredictable ways. Test extensively."]}]
3b9:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From Player Types:"}]," Different players want different things. No system serves all equally. Target specific types."]}]
3ba:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From Five Components:"}]," Systems are mechanics + parameters + context + pacing + configuration. Change any component, you change the experience."]}]
3bb:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From Core Loops:"}]," The smallest repeatable cycle must be satisfying. Tasks end, loops continue. Every element should enhance or protect the loop."]}]
3bc:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From Engagement Curves:"}]," Sessions have temporal shape. Hook → Onboarding → Early Mastery → Flow → Exit Hook. Get any phase wrong, lose the player."]}]
3bd:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From Flow Theory:"}]," Challenge must equal skill. Too hard = anxiety. Too easy = boredom. Just right = flow. Include recovery mechanics for frustrated players."]}]
3be:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From Investment/Payoff:"}]," Match system demands to player energy state. Same player needs different experiences when exhausted vs energized. Payoff must justify investment."]}]
3bf:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From System Functions:"}]," Systems don't just resolve—they adjudicate, manage information, generate content, persist state, encode cognition, design constraints, enable solo play. Structure and function both matter."]}]
3c0:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"From Designer Responsibility:"}]," Games create experiences that affect people. Purpose guides design. Knowledge and lived experience matter. Sometimes the right answer is \"I shouldn't make this game.\" Ethics are not optional."]}]
3c1:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"The Design Process:"}]}]
3c2:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Define purpose"}]," (what experience? why does it matter?)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Check ethical boundaries"}]," (should I make this? do I have the knowledge?)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Know target audience"}]," (player types, energy states)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Choose five components"}]," to serve experience:","\n",["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Mechanics (what players do)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Parameters (how much, how fast, how scarce)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Context (what it means)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Pacing (when things happen)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Configuration (how it all combines)"}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Design functions"}]," to enable experience:","\n",["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Adjudication (resolving uncertainty)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Information management (controlling discovery)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Content generation (creating situations)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"State persistence (remembering across time)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Cognitive encoding (shaping thinking) [if relevant]"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Constraint design (creating meaningful limitations)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Solo play procedures (if needed)"}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Identify core loop"}]," (what repeats, why it's satisfying)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Design engagement curve"}]," (hook to exit)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Tune for flow state"}]," (challenge scales with skill)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Match investment to payoff"}]," (respect player energy)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Include safety tools"}]," (X-Card, lines/veils, consent)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Test if experience emerges"}]," (playtest with target audience)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Iterate"}]," (or abandon if it doesn't work)"]}],"\n"]}]
3c3:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"The Core Insight:"}]}]
3c4:["$","p",null,{"children":"Systems that fail start with mechanics and look for uses. Systems that succeed start with experience and build mechanics to serve it."}]
3c5:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Good systems know:"}]}]
3c6:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"What they are (identity)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Why they exist (purpose)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Who they're for (player type and energy state)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"What they do (functions they perform)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"What boundaries they respect (ethics)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Every component serves the same aesthetic"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Every function enables the intended experience"}],"\n"]}]
3c7:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Bad systems:"}]}]
3c8:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Start with mechanics instead of aesthetics"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Add complexity without purpose"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Treat context as cosmetic"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Demand wrong investment level"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Have incoherent configuration"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Exploit instead of engage"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Ignore functions beyond resolution"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Cause harm through ignorance or carelessness"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Use wrong system for intended aesthetic"}],"\n"]}]
3c9:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"The art of game design is configuration:"}]," Choosing the right components and functions, combining them so they work together to consistently create the intended experience for the target audience at the appropriate investment level, while respecting ethical boundaries."]}]
3ca:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"The responsibility of game design is purpose:"}]," Understanding what experience you're creating, why it matters, who it's for, whether you should create it, and how to do so without causing harm."]}]
3cb:["$","p",null,{"children":"Purpose before mechanics. Always."}]
3cc:["$","p",null,{"children":"Function serves purpose. Always."}]
